From mingz at ele.uri.edu  Tue Feb  7 02:39:17 2006
From: mingz at ele.uri.edu (Ming Zhang)
Date: Mon, 06 Feb 2006 20:39:17 -0500
Subject: [Stgt-devel] any update on more target mode support?
Message-ID: <1139276357.28852.25.camel@localhost.localdomain>

Hi folks

I wonder if there is any update about supporting other type of
transport, like qlogic or lsi fc/sas?

Also I wonder if you have interest to introduce a plugin structure for
different type of virtual devices. i believe many people will have
interest to see more device type support beside disk. so if you can
define that interface, people can begin to do development in parallel.

thanks.

Ming

Seems tgt and ibmvstgt (IBM VIO server LLD) can work nicely. Now I
manage to install SUSE9 to ibmvstgt's LU, boot a client with it,
perform heavy I/Os.

The README file includes the detailed instructions. So everything is
ready.

There are still some TODOs in kernel-space tgt code, however, not
many. Most of TODOs are about user-space tgt code and LLDs.

I will write up TODOs in the project wiki site later on.


You can get the tgt code:

svn checkout http://svn.berlios.de/svnroot/repos/stgt/branches/use-scsi-ml
